\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00188}\mbox{\hyperlink{openMTPK__wrap_8c_a1a125b0e9c551bb9cdeb21b8e5be5b57}{00188}} \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define SWIG\_POINTER\_OWN           0x1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00189}00189 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00190}00190 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00191}00191 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00192}00192 \textcolor{comment}{   Flags/methods for returning states.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00193}00193 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00194}00194 \textcolor{comment}{   The SWIG conversion methods, as ConvertPtr, return an integer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00195}00195 \textcolor{comment}{   that tells if the conversion was successful or not. And if not,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00196}00196 \textcolor{comment}{   an error code can be returned (see swigerrors.swg for the codes).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00197}00197 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00198}00198 \textcolor{comment}{   Use the following macros/flags to set or process the returning}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00199}00199 \textcolor{comment}{   states.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00200}00200 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00201}00201 \textcolor{comment}{   In old versions of SWIG, code such as the following was usually written:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00202}00202 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00203}00203 \textcolor{comment}{     if (SWIG\_ConvertPtr(obj,vptr,ty.flags) != -\/1) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00204}00204 \textcolor{comment}{       // success code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00205}00205 \textcolor{comment}{     \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00206}00206 \textcolor{comment}{       //fail code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00207}00207 \textcolor{comment}{     \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00208}00208 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00209}00209 \textcolor{comment}{   Now you can be more explicit:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00210}00210 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00211}00211 \textcolor{comment}{    int res = SWIG\_ConvertPtr(obj,vptr,ty.flags);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00212}00212 \textcolor{comment}{    if (SWIG\_IsOK(res)) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00213}00213 \textcolor{comment}{      // success code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00214}00214 \textcolor{comment}{    \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00215}00215 \textcolor{comment}{      // fail code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00216}00216 \textcolor{comment}{    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00217}00217 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00218}00218 \textcolor{comment}{   which is the same really, but now you can also do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00219}00219 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00220}00220 \textcolor{comment}{    Type *ptr;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00221}00221 \textcolor{comment}{    int res = SWIG\_ConvertPtr(obj,(void **)(\&ptr),ty.flags);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00222}00222 \textcolor{comment}{    if (SWIG\_IsOK(res)) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00223}00223 \textcolor{comment}{      // success code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00224}00224 \textcolor{comment}{      if (SWIG\_IsNewObj(res) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00225}00225 \textcolor{comment}{        ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00226}00226 \textcolor{comment}{    delete *ptr;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00227}00227 \textcolor{comment}{      \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00228}00228 \textcolor{comment}{        ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00229}00229 \textcolor{comment}{      \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00230}00230 \textcolor{comment}{    \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00231}00231 \textcolor{comment}{      // fail code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00232}00232 \textcolor{comment}{    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00233}00233 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00234}00234 \textcolor{comment}{   I.e., now SWIG\_ConvertPtr can return new objects and you can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00235}00235 \textcolor{comment}{   identify the case and take care of the deallocation. Of course that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00236}00236 \textcolor{comment}{   also requires SWIG\_ConvertPtr to return new result values, such as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00237}00237 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00238}00238 \textcolor{comment}{      int SWIG\_ConvertPtr(obj, ptr,...) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00239}00239 \textcolor{comment}{        if (<obj is ok>) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00240}00240 \textcolor{comment}{          if (<need new object>) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00241}00241 \textcolor{comment}{            *ptr = <ptr to new allocated object>;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00242}00242 \textcolor{comment}{            return SWIG\_NEWOBJ;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00243}00243 \textcolor{comment}{          \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00244}00244 \textcolor{comment}{            *ptr = <ptr to old object>;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00245}00245 \textcolor{comment}{            return SWIG\_OLDOBJ;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00246}00246 \textcolor{comment}{          \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00247}00247 \textcolor{comment}{        \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00248}00248 \textcolor{comment}{          return SWIG\_BADOBJ;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00249}00249 \textcolor{comment}{        \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00250}00250 \textcolor{comment}{      \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00251}00251 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00252}00252 \textcolor{comment}{   Of course, returning the plain '0(success)/-\/1(fail)' still works, but you can be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00253}00253 \textcolor{comment}{   more explicit by returning SWIG\_BADOBJ, SWIG\_ERROR or any of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00254}00254 \textcolor{comment}{   SWIG errors code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00255}00255 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00256}00256 \textcolor{comment}{   Finally, if the SWIG\_CASTRANK\_MODE is enabled, the result code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00257}00257 \textcolor{comment}{   allows returning the 'cast rank', for example, if you have this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00258}00258 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00259}00259 \textcolor{comment}{       int food(double)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00260}00260 \textcolor{comment}{       int fooi(int);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00261}00261 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00262}00262 \textcolor{comment}{   and you call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00263}00263 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00264}00264 \textcolor{comment}{      food(1)   // cast rank '1'  (1 -\/> 1.0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00265}00265 \textcolor{comment}{      fooi(1)   // cast rank '0'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00266}00266 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00267}00267 \textcolor{comment}{   just use the SWIG\_AddCast()/SWIG\_CheckState()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00268}00268 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00269}00269 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00270}\mbox{\hyperlink{openMTPK__wrap_8c_af9ecbac56d4c5cd6104ae8f6bb82e9f7}{00270}} \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define SWIG\_OK                    (0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00271}00271 \textcolor{comment}{/* Runtime errors are < 0 */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00274}00274 \textcolor{comment}{/* Errors in range -\/100 to -\/199 are language specific errors defined in *errors.swg */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l00275}00275 \textcolor{comment}{/* Errors < -\/200 are generic runtime specific errors */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02628}02628 \textcolor{comment}{/* -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ TYPE CONVERSION AND EQUIVALENCE RULES (END) -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02629}02629 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02630}\mbox{\hyperlink{openMTPK__wrap_8c_a669d045dcc44367387d0813b82f8a7ae}{02630}} \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define SWIG\_init f\_openMTPK\_init}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02631}02631 \textcolor{comment}{/* -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02632}02632 \textcolor{comment}{ * Type initialization:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02633}02633 \textcolor{comment}{ * This problem is tough by the requirement that no dynamic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02634}02634 \textcolor{comment}{ * memory is used. Also, since swig\_type\_info structures store pointers to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02635}02635 \textcolor{comment}{ * swig\_cast\_info structures and swig\_cast\_info structures store pointers back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02636}02636 \textcolor{comment}{ * to swig\_type\_info structures, we need some lookup code at initialization.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02637}02637 \textcolor{comment}{ * The idea is that swig generates all the structures that are needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02638}02638 \textcolor{comment}{ * The runtime then collects these partially filled structures.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02639}02639 \textcolor{comment}{ * The SWIG\_InitializeModule function takes these initial arrays out of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02640}02640 \textcolor{comment}{ * swig\_module, and does all the lookup, filling in the swig\_module.types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02641}02641 \textcolor{comment}{ * array with the correct data and linking the correct swig\_cast\_info}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02642}02642 \textcolor{comment}{ * structures together.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02643}02643 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02644}02644 \textcolor{comment}{ * The generated swig\_type\_info structures are assigned statically to an initial}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02645}02645 \textcolor{comment}{ * array. We just loop through that array, and handle each type individually.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02646}02646 \textcolor{comment}{ * First we lookup if this type has been already loaded, and if so, use the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02647}02647 \textcolor{comment}{ * loaded structure instead of the generated one. Then we have to fill in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02648}02648 \textcolor{comment}{ * cast linked list. The cast data is initially stored in something like a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02649}02649 \textcolor{comment}{ * two-\/dimensional array. Each row corresponds to a type (there are the same}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02650}02650 \textcolor{comment}{ * number of rows as there are in the swig\_type\_initial array). Each entry in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02651}02651 \textcolor{comment}{ * a column is one of the swig\_cast\_info structures for that type.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02652}02652 \textcolor{comment}{ * The cast\_initial array is actually an array of arrays, because each row has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02653}02653 \textcolor{comment}{ * a variable number of columns. So to actually build the cast linked list,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02654}02654 \textcolor{comment}{ * we find the array of casts associated with the type, and loop through it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02655}02655 \textcolor{comment}{ * adding the casts to the list. The one last trick we need to do is making}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02656}02656 \textcolor{comment}{ * sure the type pointer in the swig\_cast\_info struct is correct.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02657}02657 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02658}02658 \textcolor{comment}{ * First off, we lookup the cast-\/>type name to see if it is already loaded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02659}02659 \textcolor{comment}{ * There are three cases to handle:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02660}02660 \textcolor{comment}{ *  1) If the cast-\/>type has already been loaded AND the type we are adding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02661}02661 \textcolor{comment}{ *     casting info to has not been loaded (it is in this module), THEN we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02662}02662 \textcolor{comment}{ *     replace the cast-\/>type pointer with the type pointer that has already}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02663}02663 \textcolor{comment}{ *     been loaded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02664}02664 \textcolor{comment}{ *  2) If BOTH types (the one we are adding casting info to, and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02665}02665 \textcolor{comment}{ *     cast-\/>type) are loaded, THEN the cast info has already been loaded by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02666}02666 \textcolor{comment}{ *     the previous module so we just ignore it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02667}02667 \textcolor{comment}{ *  3) Finally, if cast-\/>type has not already been loaded, then we add that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02668}02668 \textcolor{comment}{ *     swig\_cast\_info to the linked list (because the cast-\/>type) pointer will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02669}02669 \textcolor{comment}{ *     be correct.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02670}02670 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{openMTPK__wrap_8c_source_l02671}02671 }
